=== Tool Call: read ===
Args:
{
  "file_path": "colosseo.txt"
}

=== EXTRACTED CONTENT ===
The Colosseum is located in Rome, Italy. It is an iconic monument that the whole world knows. The Colosseum has baffled many with its magnificent size and grandiose built. The Colosseum today has become a must see for all who visit Rome.
The largest amphitheater ever built, the Rome Colosseum, also called the Flavian Ampitheater, is situated in the center of Rome. Built under the Flavian Dynasty, construction started in 72 AD and was completed in 80 AD. Built of concrete and sand, the Colosseum could hold up to 80,000 people, though it usually held 65,000. Spectators would come to watch gladiator contests and other spectacles for the public, such as simulated sea wars with props, public executions and mythological dramas. It wasn’t until the medieval era that the building was converted and used as a housing facility, a Christian shrine and a fortress.
The way it looks today is due to robbers stealing stones and earthquakes. In the age when the Colosseum was built, theaters were usually located on hillsides. However, the Colosseum is a free standing structure built on flat ground. Its size is 189 meters long, 156 meters wide with a base area of 24,000 square meters. The outer wall height is 48 meters. The center arena is 87 meters long and 55 meters wide with a 5-meter high barrier wall, which kept the performers inside while the audience sat above.
=== END ===

=== Tool Call: read ===
Args:
{
  "file_path": "colosseo.txt",
  "offset": 2
}

=== EXTRACTED CONTENT ===
The largest amphitheater ever built, the Rome Colosseum, also called the Flavian Ampitheater, is situated in the center of Rome. Built under the Flavian Dynasty, construction started in 72 AD and was completed in 80 AD. Built of concrete and sand, the Colosseum could hold up to 80,000 people, though it usually held 65,000. Spectators would come to watch gladiator contests and other spectacles for the public, such as simulated sea wars with props, public executions and mythological dramas. It wasn’t until the medieval era that the building was converted and used as a housing facility, a Christian shrine and a fortress.
The way it looks today is due to robbers stealing stones and earthquakes. In the age when the Colosseum was built, theaters were usually located on hillsides. However, the Colosseum is a free standing structure built on flat ground. Its size is 189 meters long, 156 meters wide with a base area of 24,000 square meters. The outer wall height is 48 meters. The center arena is 87 meters long and 55 meters wide with a 5-meter high barrier wall, which kept the performers inside while the audience sat above.
=== END ===

=== Tool Call: read ===
Args:
{
  "file_path": "colosseo.txt"
}

=== EXTRACTED CONTENT ===
The Colosseum is located in Rome, Italy. It is an iconic monument that the whole world knows. The Colosseum has baffled many with its magnificent size and grandiose built. The Colosseum today has become a must see for all who visit Rome.
The largest amphitheater ever built, the Rome Colosseum, also called the Flavian Ampitheater, is situated in the center of Rome. Built under the Flavian Dynasty, construction started in 72 AD and was completed in 80 AD. Built of concrete and sand, the Colosseum could hold up to 80,000 people, though it usually held 65,000. Spectators would come to watch gladiator contests and other spectacles for the public, such as simulated sea wars with props, public executions and mythological dramas. It wasn’t until the medieval era that the building was converted and used as a housing facility, a Christian shrine and a fortress.
The way it looks today is due to robbers stealing stones and earthquakes. In the age when the Colosseum was built, theaters were usually located on hillsides. However, the Colosseum is a free standing structure built on flat ground. Its size is 189 meters long, 156 meters wide with a base area of 24,000 square meters. The outer wall height is 48 meters. The center arena is 87 meters long and 55 meters wide with a 5-meter high barrier wall, which kept the performers inside while the audience sat above.
=== END ===

Built under the Flavian Dynasty, construction started in 72 AD and was completed in 80 AD. Built of concrete and sand, the Colosseum could hold up to 80,000 people, though it usually held 65,000. Spectators would come to watch gladiator contests and other spectacles for the public, such as simulated sea wars with props, public executions and mythological dramas. It wasn’t until the medieval era that the building was converted and used as a housing facility, a Christian shrine and a fortress.\nThe way it looks today is due to robbers stealing stones and earthquakes. Its size is 189 meters long, 156 meters wide with a base area of 24,000 square meters. The outer wall height is 48 meters. The center arena is 87 meters long and 55 meters wide with a 5-meter high barrier wall, which kept the performers inside while the audience sat above.\"\n\n***\n\n### Italian Translation:\n\"Il Colosseo si trova a Roma, Italia. È un monumento iconico che tutto il mondo conosce. Il Colosseo ha sconvolto molti con la sua magnifica dimensione e la sua grandiose costruzione. Oggi il Colosseo è diventato un must-see per tutti coloro che visitano Roma.\nL'anfiteatro più grande mai costruito, il Colosseo di Roma, anche chiamato Anfiteatro Flavio, si trova al centro di Roma. Costruito sotto la dinastia Flavia, la costruzione è iniziata nel 72 d.C. e completata nel 80 d.C. Costruito in cemento e sabbia, il Colosseo poteva ospitare fino a 80.000 persone, anche se di solito teneva 65.000. Gli spettatori venivano a vedere i combattimenti dei gladiatori e altri spettacoli per il pubblico, come guerre navali simulate con oggetti di scena, esecuzioni pubbliche e drammi mitologici. Non fu fino all'era medievale che l'edificio fu convertito e utilizzato come alloggio, santuario cristiano e fortezza.\nIl modo in cui appare oggi è dovuto ai ladri che rubavano pietre e ai terremoti. Nell'epoca in cui fu costruito il Colosseo, i teatri si trovavano di solito su pendii. Tuttavia, il Colosseo è una struttura autoportante costruita su terreno pianeggiante. Le sue dimensioni sono 189 metri di lunghezza, 156 metri di larghezza con un'area di base di 24.000 metri quadrati. L'altezza del muro esterno è di 48 metri. L'arena centrale è lunga 87 metri e larga 55 metri con un muro di barriera alto 5 metri, che teneva gli artisti all'interno mentre il pubblico sedeva sopra.\"\n\n***\n\n### German Translation:\n\"Das Kolosseum befindet sich in Rom, Italien. Es ist ein ikonisches Denkmal, von dem die ganze Welt weiß. Das Kolosseum hat viele mit seiner prächtigen Größe und seinem großartigen Bau beeindruckt. Das Kolosseum ist heute ein Muss für alle, die Rom besuchen.\nDas größte jemals gebaute Amphitheater, das Kolosseum in Rom, auch Flavianisches Amphitheater genannt, befindet sich im Zentrum von Rom. Unter der Flavianischen Dynastie begann der Bau im Jahr 72 n. Chr. und wurde im Jahr 80 n. Chr. abgeschlossen. Aus Beton und Sand gebaut, konnte das Kolosseum bis zu 80.000 Menschen aufnehmen, obwohl es normalerweise 65.000 belegte. Zuschauer kamen, um Gladiatorenkämpfe und andere Spektakel für die Öffentlichkeit zu sehen, wie simulierte Seeschlachten mit Requisiten, öffentliche Hinrichtungen und mythologische Dramen. Erst im Mittelalter wurde das Gebäude in eine Unterkunft, eine christliche Wallfahrt und eine Festung umgewandelt.\nDie Art und Weise, wie es heute aussieht, liegt an Dieben, die Steine stahlen, und an Erdbeben. In der Zeit, als das Kolosseum gebaut wurde, befanden sich Theater normalerweise auf Hängen. Das Kolosseum ist jedoch eine freistehende Struktur, die auf ebenem Boden gebaut wurde. Seine Größe beträgt 189 Meter lang, 156 Meter breit mit einer Grundfläche von 24.000 Quadratmetern. Die Höhe der äußeren Mauer beträgt 48 Meter. Die zentrale Arena ist 87 Meter lang und 55 Meter breit mit einer 5 Meter hohen Barrierewand, die die Darsteller im Inneren hielt, während das Publikum darüber saß.\""

It wasn’t until the medieval era that the building was converted and used as a housing facility, a Christian shrine and a fortress.\nThe way it looks today is due to robbers stealing stones and earthquakes. In the age when the Colosseum was built, theaters were usually located on hillsides. However, the Colosseum is a free standing structure built on flat ground. Its size is 189 meters long, 156 meters wide with a base area of 24,000 square meters. The outer wall height is 48 meters. The center arena is 87 meters long and 55 meters wide with a 5-meter high barrier wall, which kept the performers inside while the audience sat above.\""

It is an iconic monument that the whole world knows. The Colosseum has baffled many with its magnificent size and grandiose built. The Colosseum today has become a must see for all who visit Rome.\nThe largest amphitheater ever built, the Rome Colosseum, also called the Flavian Ampitheater, is situated in the center of Rome. Built under the Flavian Dynasty, construction started in 72 AD and was completed in 80 AD. Built of concrete and sand, the Colosseum could hold up to 80,000 people, though it usually held 65,000. Spectators would come to watch gladiator contests and other spectacles for the public, such as simulated sea wars with props, public executions and mythological dramas. It wasn’t until the medieval era that the building was converted and used as a housing facility, a Christian shrine and a fortress.\nThe way it looks today is due to robbers stealing stones and earthquakes. In the age when the Colosseum was built, theaters were usually located on hillsides. However, the Colosseum is a free standing structure built on flat ground. Its size is 189 meters long, 156 meters wide with a base area of 24,000 square meters. The outer wall height is 48 meters. The center arena is 87 meters long and 55 meters wide with a 5-meter high barrier wall, which kept the performers inside while the audience sat above.\"\n\n***\n\n### Italian Translation:\n\"Il Colosseo si trova a Roma, Italia. È un monumento iconico che tutto il mondo conosce. Il Colosseo ha sconvolto molti con la sua magnifica dimensione e la sua grandiose costruzione. Oggi il Colosseo è diventato un must-see per tutti coloro che visitano Roma.\nL'anfiteatro più grande mai costruito, il Colosseo di Roma, anche chiamato Anfiteatro Flavio, si trova al centro di Roma. Costruito sotto la dinastia Flavia, la costruzione è iniziata nel 72 d.C. e completata nel 80 d.C. Costruito in cemento e sabbia, il Colosseo poteva ospitare fino a 80.000 persone, anche se di solito teneva 65.000. Gli spettatori venivano a vedere i combattimenti dei gladiatori e altri spettacoli per il pubblico, come guerre navali simulate con oggetti di scena, esecuzioni pubbliche e drammi mitologici. Non fu fino all'era medievale che l'edificio fu convertito e utilizzato come alloggio, santuario cristiano e fortezza.\nIl modo in cui appare oggi è dovuto ai ladri che rubavano pietre e ai terremoti. Nell'epoca in cui fu costruito il Colosseo, i teatri si trovavano di solito su pendii. Tuttavia, il Colosseo è una struttura autoportante costruita su terreno pianeggiante. Le sue dimensioni sono 189 metri di lunghezza, 156 metri di larghezza con un'area di base di 24.000 metri quadrati. L'altezza del muro esterno è di 48 metri. L'arena centrale è lunga 87 metri e larga 55 metri con un muro di barriera alto 5 metri, che teneva gli artisti all'interno mentre il pubblico sedeva sopra.\"\n\n***\n\n### German Translation:\n\"Das Kolosseum befindet sich in Rom, Italien. Es ist ein ikonisches Denkmal, von dem die ganze Welt weiß. Das Kolosseum hat viele mit seiner prächtigen Größe und seinem großartigen Bau beeindruckt. Das Kolosseum ist heute ein Muss für alle, die Rom besuchen.\nDas größte jemals gebaute Amphitheater, das Kolosseum in Rom, auch Flavianisches Amphitheater genannt, befindet sich im Zentrum von Rom. Unter der Flavianischen Dynastie begann der Bau im Jahr 72 n. Chr. und wurde im Jahr 80 n. Chr. abgeschlossen. Aus Beton und Sand gebaut, konnte das Kolosseum bis zu 80.000 Menschen aufnehmen, obwohl es normalerweise 65.000 belegte. Zuschauer kamen, um Gladiatorenkämpfe und andere Spektakel für die Öffentlichkeit zu sehen, wie simulierte Seeschlachten mit Requisiten, öffentliche Hinrichtungen und mythologische Dramen. Erst im Mittelalter wurde das Gebäude in eine Unterkunft, eine christliche Wallfahrt und eine Festung umgewandelt.\nDie Art und Weise, wie es heute aussieht, liegt an Dieben, die Steine stahlen, und an Erdbeben. In der Zeit, als das Kolosseum gebaut wurde, befanden sich Theater normalerweise auf Hängen. Das Kolosseum ist jedoch eine freistehende Struktur, die auf ebenem Boden gebaut wurde. Seine Größe beträgt 189 Meter lang, 156 Meter breit mit einer Grundfläche von 24.000 Quadratmetern. Die Höhe der äußeren Mauer beträgt 48 Meter. Die zentrale Arena ist 87 Meter lang und 55 Meter breit mit einer 5 Meter hohen Barrierewand, die die Darsteller im Inneren hielt, während das Publikum darüber saß.\""

=== Tool Call: read ===
Args:
{
  "file_path": "colosseo.txt"
}

=== EXTRACTED CONTENT ===
The Colosseum is located in Rome, Italy. It is an iconic monument that the whole world knows. The Colosseum has baffled many with its magnificent size and grandiose built. The Colosseum today has become a must see for all who visit Rome.
The largest amphitheater ever built, the Rome Colosseum, also called the Flavian Ampitheater, is situated in the center of Rome. Built under the Flavian Dynasty, construction started in 72 AD and was completed in 80 AD. Built of concrete and sand, the Colosseum could hold up to 80,000 people, though it usually held 65,000. Spectators would come to watch gladiator contests and other spectacles for the public, such as simulated sea wars with props, public executions and mythological dramas. It wasn’t until the medieval era that the building was converted and used as a housing facility, a Christian shrine and a fortress.
The way it looks today is due to robbers stealing stones and earthquakes. In the age when the Colosseum was built, theaters were usually located on hillsides. However, the Colosseum is a free standing structure built on flat ground. Its size is 189 meters long, 156 meters wide with a base area of 24,000 square meters. The outer wall height is 48 meters. The center arena is 87 meters long and 55 meters wide with a 5-meter high barrier wall, which kept the performers inside while the audience sat above.
=== END ===

=== Tool Call: read ===
Args:
{
  "file_path": "colosseo.txt",
  "offset": 1,
  "limit": 10
}

=== EXTRACTED CONTENT ===
The Colosseum is located in Rome, Italy. It is an iconic monument that the whole world knows. The Colosseum has baffled many with its magnificent size and grandiose built. The Colosseum today has become a must see for all who visit Rome.
The largest amphitheater ever built, the Rome Colosseum, also called the Flavian Ampitheater, is situated in the center of Rome. Built under the Flavian Dynasty, construction started in 72 AD and was completed in 80 AD. Built of concrete and sand, the Colosseum could hold up to 80,000 people, though it usually held 65,000. Spectators would come to watch gladiator contests and other spectacles for the public, such as simulated sea wars with props, public executions and mythological dramas. It wasn’t until the medieval era that the building was converted and used as a housing facility, a Christian shrine and a fortress.
The way it looks today is due to robbers stealing stones and earthquakes. In the age when the Colosseum was built, theaters were usually located on hillsides. However, the Colosseum is a free standing structure built on flat ground. Its size is 189 meters long, 156 meters wide with a base area of 24,000 square meters. The outer wall height is 48 meters. The center arena is 87 meters long and 55 meters wide with a 5-meter high barrier wall, which kept the performers inside while the audience sat above.
=== END ===

The Colosseum is located in Rome, Italy. It is an iconic monument that the whole world knows. The Colosseum has baffled many with its magnificent size and grandiose built. The Colosseum today has become a must see for all who visit Rome.
The largest amphitheater ever built, the Rome Colosseum, also called the Flavian Ampitheater, is situated in the center of Rome. Built under the Flavian Dynasty, construction started in 72 AD and was completed in 80 AD. Built of concrete and sand, the Colosseum could hold up to 80,000 people, though it usually held 65,000. Spectators would come to watch gladiator contests and other spectacles for the public, such as simulated sea wars with props, public executions and mythological dramas. It wasn’t until the medieval era that the building was converted and used as a housing facility, a Christian shrine and a fortress.
The way it looks today is due to robbers stealing stones and earthquakes. In the age when the Colosseum was built, theaters were usually located on hillsides. However, the Colosseum is a free standing structure built on flat ground. Its size is 189 meters long, 156 meters wide with a base area of 24,000 square meters. The outer wall height is 48 meters. The center arena is 87 meters long and 55 meters wide with a 5-meter high barrier wall, which kept the performers inside while the audience sat above.
=== END ===

=== Tool Call: read ===
Args:
{
  "file_path": "colosseo.txt"
}

=== EXTRACTED CONTENT ===
The Colosseum is located in Rome, Italy. It is an iconic monument that the whole world knows. The Colosseum has baffled many with its magnificent size and grandiose built. The Colosseum today has become a must see for all who visit Rome.
The largest amphitheater ever built, the Rome Colosseum, also called the Flavian Ampitheater, is situated in the center of Rome. Built under the Flavian Dynasty, construction started in 72 AD and was completed in 80 AD. Built of concrete and sand, the Colosseum could hold up to 80,000 people, though it usually held 65,000. Spectators would come to watch gladiator contests and other spectacles for the public, such as simulated sea wars with props, public executions and mythological dramas. It wasn’t until the medieval era that the building was converted and used as a housing facility, a Christian shrine and a fortress.
The way it looks today is due to robbers stealing stones and earthquakes. In the age when the Colosseum was built, theaters were usually located on hillsides. However, the Colosseum is a free standing structure built on flat ground. Its size is 189 meters long, 156 meters wide with a base area of 24,000 square meters. The outer wall height is 48 meters. The center arena is 87 meters long and 55 meters wide with a 5-meter high barrier wall, which kept the performers inside while the audience sat above.
=== END ===

=== Tool Call: bash ===
Args:
{
  "command": "cat colosseo.txt"
}

=== EXTRACTED CONTENT ===
The Colosseum is located in Rome, Italy. It is an iconic monument that the whole world knows. The Colosseum has baffled many with its magnificent size and grandiose built. The Colosseum today has become a must see for all who visit Rome.
The largest amphitheater ever built, the Rome Colosseum, also called the Flavian Ampitheater, is situated in the center of Rome. Built under the Flavian Dynasty, construction started in 72 AD and was completed in 80 AD. Built of concrete and sand, the Colosseum could hold up to 80,000 people, though it usually held 65,000. Spectators would come to watch gladiator contests and other spectacles for the public, such as simulated sea wars with props, public executions and mythological dramas. It wasn’t until the medieval era that the building was converted and used as a housing facility, a Christian shrine and a fortress.
The way it looks today is due to robbers stealing stones and earthquakes. In the age when the Colosseum was built, theaters were usually located on hillsides. However, the Colosseum is a free standing structure built on flat ground. Its size is 189 meters long, 156 meters wide with a base area of 24,000 square meters. The outer wall height is 48 meters. The center arena is 87 meters long and 55 meters wide with a 5-meter high barrier wall, which kept the performers inside while the audience sat above.
=== END ===

=== EXTRACTED CONTENT ===
The Colosseum is located in Rome, Italy. It is an iconic monument that the whole world knows. The Colosseum has baffled many with its magnificent size and grandiose built. The Colosseum today has become a must see for all who visit Rome.
The largest amphitheater ever built, the Rome Colosseum, also called the Flavian Ampitheater, is situated in the center of Rome. Built under the Flavian Dynasty, construction started in 72 AD and was completed in 80 AD. Built of concrete and sand, the Colosseum could hold up to 80,000 people, though it usually held 65,000. Spectators would come to watch gladiator contests and other spectacles for the public, such as simulated sea wars with props, public executions and mythological dramas. It wasn’t until the medieval era that the building was converted and used as a housing facility, a Christian shrine and a fortress.
The way it looks today is due to robbers stealing stones and earthquakes. In the age when the Colosseum was built, theaters were usually located on hillsides. However, the Colosseum is a free standing structure built on flat ground. Its size is 189 meters long, 156 meters wide with a base area of 24,000 square meters. The outer wall height is 48 meters. The center arena is 87 meters long and 55 meters wide with a 5-meter high barrier wall, which kept the performers inside while the audience sat above.
=== END ===

The Colosseum today has become a must see for all who visit Rome.\nThe largest amphitheater ever built, the Rome Colosseum, also called the Flavian Ampitheater, is situated in the center of Rome. Built under the Flavian Dynasty, construction started in 72 AD and was completed in 80 AD. Built of concrete and sand, the Colosseum could hold up to 80,000 people, though it usually held 65,000. Spectators would come to watch gladiator contests and other spectacles for the public, such as simulated sea wars with props, public executions and mythological dramas. It wasn’t until the medieval era that the building was converted and used as a housing facility, a Christian shrine and a fortress.\nThe way it looks today is due to robbers stealing stones and earthquakes. In the age when the Colosseum was built, theaters were usually located on hillsides. However, the Colosseum is a free standing structure built on flat ground. Its size is 189 meters long, 156 meters wide with a base area of 24,000 square meters. The outer wall height is 48 meters. The center arena is 87 meters long and 55 meters wide with a 5-meter high barrier wall, which kept the performers inside while the audience sat above."

Construit sous la dynastie Flavienne, la construction a commencé en 72 après J.-C. et a été achevée en 80 après J.-C. À l'époque de sa construction, les théâtres étaient généralement situés sur des pentes. Cependant, le Colisée est une structure debout construite sur un terrain plat. Sa taille est de 189 mètres de long, 156 mètres de large avec une aire de base de 24 000 mètres carrés. La hauteur de la muraille extérieure est de 48 mètres. The Colosseum today has become a must see for all who visit Rome.\nThe largest amphitheater ever built, the Rome Colosseum, also called the Flavian Ampitheater, is situated in the center of Rome. Built under the Flavian Dynasty, construction started in 72 AD and was completed in 80 AD. Built of concrete and sand, the Colosseum could hold up to 80,000 people, though it usually held 65,000. Spectators would come to watch gladiator contests and other spectacles for the public, such as simulated sea wars with props, public executions and mythological dramas. It wasn’t until the medieval era that the building was converted and used as a housing facility, a Christian shrine and a fortress.\nThe way it looks today is due to robbers stealing stones and earthquakes. In the age when the Colosseum was built, theaters were usually located on hillsides. However, the Colosseum is a free standing structure built on flat ground. Its size is 189 meters long, 156 meters wide with a base area of 24,000 square meters. The outer wall height is 48 meters. The center arena is 87 meters long and 55 meters wide with a 5-meter high barrier wall, which kept the performers inside while the audience sat above."

Construit sous la dynastie Flavienne, la construction a commencé en 72 après J.-C. et a été achevée en 80 après J.-C. Conçu en béton et sable, le Colisée pouvait accueillir jusqu'à 80 000 personnes, bien qu'il accueille généralement 65 000. Les spectateurs y venaient assister à des combats de gladiateurs et à d'autres spectacles publics, tels que des simulations de guerres maritimes avec des accessoires, des exécutions publiques et des drames mythologiques. Ce n'est qu'à l'époque médiévale que le bâtiment a été transformé et utilisé comme logement, sanctuaire chrétien et fortification.\n\nL'apparence actuelle du Colisée est due aux voleurs qui ont dérobé des pierres et aux tremblements de terre. À l'époque de sa construction, les théâtres étaient généralement situés sur des pentes. Cependant, le Colisée est une structure debout construite sur un terrain plat. Sa taille est de 189 mètres de long, 156 mètres de large avec une aire de base de 24 000 mètres carrés. La hauteur de la muraille extérieure est de 48 mètres. Les spectateurs y venaient assister à des combats de gladiateurs et à d'autres spectacles publics, tels que des simulations de guerres maritimes avec des accessoires, des exécutions publiques et des drames mythologiques. Ce n'est qu'à l'époque médiévale que le bâtiment a été transformé et utilisé comme logement, sanctuaire chrétien et fortification.\n\nL'apparence actuelle du Colisée est due aux voleurs qui ont dérobé des pierres et aux tremblements de terre. À l'époque de sa construction, les théâtres étaient généralement situés sur des pentes. Cependant, le Colisée est une structure debout construite sur un terrain plat. Sa taille est de 189 mètres de long, 156 mètres de large avec une aire de base de 24 000 mètres carrés. La hauteur de la muraille extérieure est de 48 mètres. La cour centrale mesure 87 mètres de long et 55 mètres de large, avec une barrière de 5 mètres de haut qui retenait les performers tandis que le public était au-dessus.\n\n---\n\nN'hésitez pas si vous avez besoin d'autres traductions ou d'informations supplémentaires !"
